**Facilities: It can be seen that it has been in business for a while, the focus is on how to maintain the facilities, and the maintenance work is still in place.
But the location is really great, the outdoor garden on the 6th floor is my favorite. Go for a walk in the outdoor garden at night and enjoy the "grace" of the small waist. The West Tower is close at hand, and I am deeply attracted by this beautiful night scene...
**Breakfast: There are hot and cold dishes and specialty stalls. The variety is not very rich.
All in all, it is recommended for those who care about cost performance!
